47→  if (!rule.cookie().empty() && !rule.header().empty()) {\n    48→    throw EnvoyException(\"Cannot specify both header and cookie\");\n    49→  }\n    50→\n    51→  // Initialize the shared pointer.\n    52→  if (!rule.header().empty()) {\n    53→    selector_ =\n    54→        std::make_shared<HeaderValueSelector>(Http::LowerCaseString(rule.header()), rule.remove());\n    55→  } else if    const auto& error = fmt::format(\"header to metadata filter: rule for {} has neither \"\n    64→                                    \"`on_header_present` nor `on_header_missing` set\",\n    65→                                    selector_->toString());\n    66→    throw EnvoyException(error);\n    67→  }\n    68→\n    69→  // Ensure value and regex_value_rewrite are not mixed.\n    70→  // TODO(rgs1): remove this once we are on v4 and these fields are folded into a oneof.\n    71→  if (!rule.on_header_present().value().empty() &&\n    72→      rule.on_header_present().has_regex_value_rewrite()) {\n    73→    throw EnvoyException(\"Cannot specify both value and regex_value_rewrite\");\n    74→  }\n    75→\n    76→  // Remove field is 85→  if (rule.on_header_present().has_regex_value_rewrite()) {\n    86→    const auto& rewrite_spec = rule.on_header_present().regex_value_rewrite();\n    87→    regex_rewrite_ =\n    88→ rewrite_spec.substitution();\n    91→  }\n    92→}\n    93→\n    94→Config::Config(const envoy::extensions::filters::http::header_to_metadata::v3::Config config,\n    95→               Regex::Engine&
